\subsection{Detailed Description}
Author\-: Matthew Horridge\par
 The University Of Manchester\par
 Bio-\/\-Health Informatics Group Date\-: 24-\/\-Oct-\/2006 

An interface for creating entities, class expressions and axioms. All methods throw Illegal\-Argument\-Exception if null values are passed where they are not allowed in the documentation.

Gets an annotation assertion that specifies that an \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} is deprecated. The annotation property is owl\-:deprecated and the value of the annotation is {\ttfamily \char`\"{}true\char`\"{}$^\wedge$$^\wedge$xsd\-:boolean}. (See \href{http://www.w3.org/TR/2009/REC-owl2-syntax-20091027/#Annotation_Properties}{\tt Annotation Properties} in the O\-W\-L 2 Specification


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em subject} & The \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} to be deprecated. Cannot be null. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\hypertarget{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_data_factory_ae64e0cd2aba48299a7add16d4e254f81}{\index{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Data\-Factory@{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Data\-Factory}!get\-O\-W\-L\-Annotation\-Property@{get\-O\-W\-L\-Annotation\-Property}}
\index{get\-O\-W\-L\-Annotation\-Property@{get\-O\-W\-L\-Annotation\-Property}!org::semanticweb::owlapi::model::OWLDataFactory@{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Data\-Factory}}
\subsubsection[{get\-O\-W\-L\-Annotation\-Property}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf O\-W\-L\-Annotation\-Property} org.\-semanticweb.\-owlapi.\-model.\-O\-W\-L\-Data\-Factory.\-get\-O\-W\-L\-Annotation\-Property (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{String}]{abbreviated\-I\-R\-I, }
\item[{{\bf Prefix\-Manager}}]{prefix\-Manager}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_data_factory_ae64e0cd2aba48299a7add16d4e254f81}
Gets an \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_annotation_property}{O\-W\-L\-Annotation\-Property} that has an \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} that is obtained by expanding an abbreviated name using an appropriate prefix mapping. See \href{http://www.w3.org/TR/2009/REC-owl2-syntax-20091027/#IRIs}{\tt The O\-W\-L 2 Structural Specification} for more details.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em abbreviated\-I\-R\-I} & The abbreviated \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I}, which is of the form P\-R\-E\-F\-I\-X\-\_\-\-N\-A\-M\-E\-:R\-C, where P\-R\-E\-F\-I\-X\-\_\-\-N\-A\-M\-E may be the empty string (the default prefix). Note that abbreviated I\-R\-Is always contain a colon as a delimiter, even if the prefix name is the empty string. Cannot be null. \\
\hline
{\em prefix\-Manager} & The prefix manager that is responsible for mapping prefix names to prefix I\-R\-Is. Cannot be null. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
An \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_annotation_property}{O\-W\-L\-Annotation\-Property} that has the \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} obtained by expanding the specified abbreviated \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} using the specified prefix manager. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
For example, suppose \char`\"{}m\-:\-Cat\char`\"{} was specified as the abbreviated \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I}, the prefix manager would be used to obtain the \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} prefix for the \char`\"{}m\-:\char`\"{} prefix name, this prefix would then be concatenated with \char`\"{}\-Cat\char`\"{} to obtain the full \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} which would be the \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} of the \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_annotation_property}{O\-W\-L\-Annotation\-Property} obtained by this method. 
\begin{DoxyExceptions}{Exceptions}
{\em \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_runtime_exception}{O\-W\-L\-Runtime\-Exception}} & if the prefix name in the specified abbreviated \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} does not have a mapping to a prefix in the specified prefix manager. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyExceptions}

\hypertarget{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_data_factory_a0ac82c5c8f0497b26b1d4060704e8a49}{\index{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Data\-Factory@{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Data\-Factory}!get\-O\-W\-L\-Class@{get\-O\-W\-L\-Class}}
\index{get\-O\-W\-L\-Class@{get\-O\-W\-L\-Class}!org::semanticweb::owlapi::model::OWLDataFactory@{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Data\-Factory}}
\subsubsection[{get\-O\-W\-L\-Class}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf O\-W\-L\-Class} org.\-semanticweb.\-owlapi.\-model.\-O\-W\-L\-Data\-Factory.\-get\-O\-W\-L\-Class (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{String}]{abbreviated\-I\-R\-I, }
\item[{{\bf Prefix\-Manager}}]{prefix\-Manager}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_data_factory_a0ac82c5c8f0497b26b1d4060704e8a49}
Gets an \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_class}{O\-W\-L\-Class} that has an \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} that is obtained by expanding an abbreviated name using an appropriate prefix mapping. See \href{http://www.w3.org/TR/2009/REC-owl2-syntax-20091027/#IRIs}{\tt The O\-W\-L 2 Structural Specification} for more details.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em abbreviated\-I\-R\-I} & The abbreviated \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I}, which is of the form P\-R\-E\-F\-I\-X\-\_\-\-N\-A\-M\-E\-:R\-C, where P\-R\-E\-F\-I\-X\-\_\-\-N\-A\-M\-E may be the empty string (the default prefix). Cannot be null. Note that abbreviated I\-R\-Is always contain a colon as a delimiter, even if the prefix name is the empty string. \\
\hline
{\em prefix\-Manager} & The prefix manager that is responsible for mapping prefix names to prefix I\-R\-Is. Cannot be null. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
An \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_class}{O\-W\-L\-Class} that has the \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} obtained by expanding the specified abbreviated \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} using the specified prefix manager. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
For example, suppose \char`\"{}m\-:\-Cat\char`\"{} was specified as the abbreviated \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I}, the prefix manager would be used to obtain the \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} prefix for the \char`\"{}m\-:\char`\"{} prefix name, this prefix would then be concatenated with \char`\"{}\-Cat\char`\"{} to obtain the full \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} which would be the \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} of the \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_class}{O\-W\-L\-Class} obtained by this method. 
\begin{DoxyExceptions}{Exceptions}
{\em \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_runtime_exception}{O\-W\-L\-Runtime\-Exception}} & if the prefix name in the specified abbreviated \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} does not have a mapping to a prefix in the specified prefix manager. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyExceptions}

\hypertarget{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_data_factory_ab49fccef5611362b04383164ca508a51}{\index{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Data\-Factory@{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Data\-Factory}!get\-O\-W\-L\-Data\-Property@{get\-O\-W\-L\-Data\-Property}}
\index{get\-O\-W\-L\-Data\-Property@{get\-O\-W\-L\-Data\-Property}!org::semanticweb::owlapi::model::OWLDataFactory@{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Data\-Factory}}
\subsubsection[{get\-O\-W\-L\-Data\-Property}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf O\-W\-L\-Data\-Property} org.\-semanticweb.\-owlapi.\-model.\-O\-W\-L\-Data\-Factory.\-get\-O\-W\-L\-Data\-Property (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{String}]{abbreviated\-I\-R\-I, }
\item[{{\bf Prefix\-Manager}}]{prefix\-Manager}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_data_factory_ab49fccef5611362b04383164ca508a51}
Gets an \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_data_property}{O\-W\-L\-Data\-Property} that has an \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} that is obtained by expanding an abbreviated name using an appropriate prefix mapping. See \href{http://www.w3.org/TR/2009/REC-owl2-syntax-20091027/#IRIs}{\tt The O\-W\-L 2 Structural Specification} for more details.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em abbreviated\-I\-R\-I} & The abbreviated \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I}, which is of the form P\-R\-E\-F\-I\-X\-\_\-\-N\-A\-M\-E\-:R\-C, where P\-R\-E\-F\-I\-X\-\_\-\-N\-A\-M\-E may be the empty string (the default prefix). Note that abbreviated I\-R\-Is always contain a colon as a delimiter, even if the prefix name is the empty string. Cannot be null. \\
\hline
{\em prefix\-Manager} & The prefix manager that is responsible for mapping prefix names to prefix I\-R\-Is. Cannot be null. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
An \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_data_property}{O\-W\-L\-Data\-Property} that has the \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} obtained by expanding the specified abbreviated \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} using the specified prefix manager. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
For example, suppose \char`\"{}m\-:\-Cat\char`\"{} was specified as the abbreviated \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I}, the prefix manager would be used to obtain the \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} prefix for the \char`\"{}m\-:\char`\"{} prefix name, this prefix would then be concatenated with \char`\"{}\-Cat\char`\"{} to obtain the full \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} which would be the \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} of the \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_data_property}{O\-W\-L\-Data\-Property} obtained by this method. 
\begin{DoxyExceptions}{Exceptions}
{\em \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_runtime_exception}{O\-W\-L\-Runtime\-Exception}} & if the prefix name in the specified abbreviated \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} does not have a mapping to a prefix in the specified prefix manager. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyExceptions}

\hypertarget{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_data_factory_a7be1821ba6dcfb2641191938e0006a8d}{\index{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Data\-Factory@{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Data\-Factory}!get\-O\-W\-L\-Datatype@{get\-O\-W\-L\-Datatype}}
\index{get\-O\-W\-L\-Datatype@{get\-O\-W\-L\-Datatype}!org::semanticweb::owlapi::model::OWLDataFactory@{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Data\-Factory}}
\subsubsection[{get\-O\-W\-L\-Datatype}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf O\-W\-L\-Datatype} org.\-semanticweb.\-owlapi.\-model.\-O\-W\-L\-Data\-Factory.\-get\-O\-W\-L\-Datatype (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{String}]{abbreviated\-I\-R\-I, }
\item[{{\bf Prefix\-Manager}}]{prefix\-Manager}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_data_factory_a7be1821ba6dcfb2641191938e0006a8d}
Gets an \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_datatype}{O\-W\-L\-Datatype} that has an \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} that is obtained by expanding an abbreviated name using an appropriate prefix mapping. See \href{http://www.w3.org/TR/2009/REC-owl2-syntax-20091027/#IRIs}{\tt The O\-W\-L 2 Structural Specification} for more details.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em abbreviated\-I\-R\-I} & The abbreviated \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I}, which is of the form P\-R\-E\-F\-I\-X\-\_\-\-N\-A\-M\-E\-:R\-C, where P\-R\-E\-F\-I\-X\-\_\-\-N\-A\-M\-E may be the empty string (the default prefix). Note that abbreviated I\-R\-Is always contain a colon as a delimiter, even if the prefix name is the empty string. Cannot be null. \\
\hline
{\em prefix\-Manager} & The prefix manager that is responsible for mapping prefix names to prefix I\-R\-Is. Cannot be null. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
An \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_datatype}{O\-W\-L\-Datatype} that has the \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} obtained by expanding the specified abbreviated \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} using the specified prefix manager. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
For example, suppose \char`\"{}m\-:\-Cat\char`\"{} was specified as the abbreviated \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I}, the prefix manager would be used to obtain the \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} prefix for the \char`\"{}m\-:\char`\"{} prefix name, this prefix would then be concatenated with \char`\"{}\-Cat\char`\"{} to obtain the full \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} which would be the \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} of the \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_datatype}{O\-W\-L\-Datatype} obtained by this method. 
\begin{DoxyExceptions}{Exceptions}
{\em \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_runtime_exception}{O\-W\-L\-Runtime\-Exception}} & if the prefix name in the specified abbreviated \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} does not have a mapping to a prefix in the specified prefix manager. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyExceptions}

\hline
{\em datatype} & The datatype. Cannot be null. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
An \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_literal}{O\-W\-L\-Literal} with the specified lexical value and specified datatype. If the datatype is {\ttfamily rdf\-:Plain\-Literal}, and the lexical value contains a language tag then the language tag will be parsed out of the lexical value. For example, \char`\"{}abc@en\char`\"{}$^\wedge$$^\wedge$rdf\-:Plain\-Literal would be parsed into a lexical value of \char`\"{}abc\char`\"{} and a language tag of \char`\"{}en\char`\"{}. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\hypertarget{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_data_factory_a6981475d0ea7400e1510f7364040da80}{\index{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Data\-Factory@{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Data\-Factory}!get\-O\-W\-L\-Literal@{get\-O\-W\-L\-Literal}}
\index{get\-O\-W\-L\-Literal@{get\-O\-W\-L\-Literal}!org::semanticweb::owlapi::model::OWLDataFactory@{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Data\-Factory}}
\subsubsection[{get\-O\-W\-L\-Literal}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf O\-W\-L\-Literal} org.\-semanticweb.\-owlapi.\-model.\-O\-W\-L\-Data\-Factory.\-get\-O\-W\-L\-Literal (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{String}]{literal, }
\item[{String}]{lang}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_data_factory_a6981475d0ea7400e1510f7364040da80}
Gets an \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_literal}{O\-W\-L\-Literal} with a language tag. The datatype of this literal will have an \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} of rdf\-:Plain\-Literal ( \hyperlink{enumorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1vocab_1_1_o_w_l_r_d_f_vocabulary_a01c2f8d91e14f1b3ce7b2470bf641f50}{org.\-semanticweb.\-owlapi.\-vocab.\-O\-W\-L\-R\-D\-F\-Vocabulary\#\-R\-D\-F\-\_\-\-P\-L\-A\-I\-N\-\_\-\-L\-I\-T\-E\-R\-A\-L}).


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em literal} & The string literal. Cannot be null. \\
\hline
{\em lang} & The language tag. The empty string may be specified to indicate an empty language tag. Leading and trailing white space will be removed from the tag and the tag will be normalised to L\-O\-W\-E\-R C\-A\-S\-E. If {\ttfamily lang} is {\ttfamily null} then {\ttfamily lang} will be converted to the empty string (for backwards compatibility). If not empty, the tag is formed according to \href{http://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/bcp/bcp47.txt}{\tt B\-C\-P47} but the O\-W\-L A\-P\-I will not check that the tag conforms to this specification -\/ it is up to the caller to ensure this. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_literal}{O\-W\-L\-Literal} that represents the string literal with a (possibly empty) language tag. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\hypertarget{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_data_factory_a733241a0120824ba96226165cfc13aad}{\index{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Data\-Factory@{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Data\-Factory}!get\-O\-W\-L\-Named\-Individual@{get\-O\-W\-L\-Named\-Individual}}
\index{get\-O\-W\-L\-Named\-Individual@{get\-O\-W\-L\-Named\-Individual}!org::semanticweb::owlapi::model::OWLDataFactory@{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Data\-Factory}}
\subsubsection[{get\-O\-W\-L\-Named\-Individual}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf O\-W\-L\-Named\-Individual} org.\-semanticweb.\-owlapi.\-model.\-O\-W\-L\-Data\-Factory.\-get\-O\-W\-L\-Named\-Individual (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{String}]{abbreviated\-I\-R\-I, }
\item[{{\bf Prefix\-Manager}}]{prefix\-Manager}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_data_factory_a733241a0120824ba96226165cfc13aad}
Gets an \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_named_individual}{O\-W\-L\-Named\-Individual} that has an \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} that is obtained by expanding an abbreviated name using an appropriate prefix mapping. See \href{http://www.w3.org/TR/2009/REC-owl2-syntax-20091027/#IRIs}{\tt The O\-W\-L 2 Structural Specification} for more details.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em abbreviated\-I\-R\-I} & The abbreviated \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I}, which is of the form P\-R\-E\-F\-I\-X\-\_\-\-N\-A\-M\-E\-:R\-C, where P\-R\-E\-F\-I\-X\-\_\-\-N\-A\-M\-E may be the empty string (the default prefix). Note that abbreviated I\-R\-Is always contain a colon as a delimiter, even if the prefix name is the empty string. Cannot be null. \\
\hline
{\em prefix\-Manager} & The prefix manager that is responsible for mapping prefix names to prefix I\-R\-Is. Cannot be null. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
An \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_named_individual}{O\-W\-L\-Named\-Individual} that has the \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} obtained by expanding the specified abbreviated \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} using the specified prefix manager. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
For example, suppose \char`\"{}m\-:\-Cat\char`\"{} was specified as the abbreviated \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I}, the prefix manager would be used to obtain the \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} prefix for the \char`\"{}m\-:\char`\"{} prefix name, this prefix would then be concatenated with \char`\"{}\-Cat\char`\"{} to obtain the full \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} which would be the \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} of the \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_named_individual}{O\-W\-L\-Named\-Individual} obtained by this method. 
\begin{DoxyExceptions}{Exceptions}
{\em \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_runtime_exception}{O\-W\-L\-Runtime\-Exception}} & if the prefix name in the specified abbreviated \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} does not have a mapping to a prefix in the specified prefix manager. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyExceptions}

\hypertarget{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_data_factory_a616b522bbf71995972b267ff1c7a40e5}{\index{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Data\-Factory@{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Data\-Factory}!get\-O\-W\-L\-Object\-Property@{get\-O\-W\-L\-Object\-Property}}
\index{get\-O\-W\-L\-Object\-Property@{get\-O\-W\-L\-Object\-Property}!org::semanticweb::owlapi::model::OWLDataFactory@{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Data\-Factory}}
\subsubsection[{get\-O\-W\-L\-Object\-Property}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf O\-W\-L\-Object\-Property} org.\-semanticweb.\-owlapi.\-model.\-O\-W\-L\-Data\-Factory.\-get\-O\-W\-L\-Object\-Property (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{String}]{abbreviated\-I\-R\-I, }
\item[{{\bf Prefix\-Manager}}]{prefix\-Manager}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_data_factory_a616b522bbf71995972b267ff1c7a40e5}
Gets an \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_object_property}{O\-W\-L\-Object\-Property} that has an \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} that is obtained by expanding an abbreviated name using an appropriate prefix mapping. See \href{http://www.w3.org/TR/2009/REC-owl2-syntax-20091027/#IRIs}{\tt The O\-W\-L 2 Structural Specification} for more details.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em abbreviated\-I\-R\-I} & The abbreviated \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I}, which is of the form P\-R\-E\-F\-I\-X\-\_\-\-N\-A\-M\-E\-:R\-C, where P\-R\-E\-F\-I\-X\-\_\-\-N\-A\-M\-E may be the empty string (the default prefix). Cannot be null. Note that abbreviated I\-R\-Is always contain a colon as a delimiter, even if the prefix name is the empty string. \\
\hline
{\em prefix\-Manager} & The prefix manager that is responsible for mapping prefix names to prefix I\-R\-Is. Cannot be null. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
An \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_object_property}{O\-W\-L\-Object\-Property} that has the \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} obtained by expanding the specified abbreviated \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} using the specified prefix manager. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
For example, suppose \char`\"{}m\-:\-Cat\char`\"{} was specified as the abbreviated \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I}, the prefix manager would be used to obtain the \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} prefix for the \char`\"{}m\-:\char`\"{} prefix name, this prefix would then be concatenated with \char`\"{}\-Cat\char`\"{} to obtain the full \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} which would be the \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} of the \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_object_property}{O\-W\-L\-Object\-Property} obtained by this method. 
\begin{DoxyExceptions}{Exceptions}
{\em \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_runtime_exception}{O\-W\-L\-Runtime\-Exception}} & if the prefix name in the specified abbreviated \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} does not have a mapping to a prefix in the specified prefix manager. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyExceptions}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em literal} & The string literal. Cannot be null. \\
\hline
{\em lang} & The language tag. The tag is formed according to \href{http://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/bcp/bcp47.txt}{\tt B\-C\-P47} but the O\-W\-L A\-P\-I will not check that the tag conforms to this specification -\/ it is up to the caller to ensure this. For backwards compatibility, if the value of lang is {\ttfamily null} then this is equivalent to calling the \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_data_factory_ab4013507f93c4919875c37108a60008c}{get\-O\-W\-L\-String\-Literal(\-String literal)} method. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The O\-W\-L\-String\-Literal that represents the string literal with a language tag. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Deprecated}
\item[\hyperlink{deprecated__deprecated000013}{Deprecated}]Use \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_data_factory_a6981475d0ea7400e1510f7364040da80}{get\-O\-W\-L\-Literal(\-String, String)} Gets an O\-W\-L\-String\-Literal with a language tag. \end{DoxyRefDesc}
